 aaj mahaan geetkaar shailendra kii berth aneverseri he

 unka puraa naam shankaradaas kesarilaal he

 is gane kaa upyog superstar dev anand kii film main kiya gaya tha

 aaj shailendra kii berth aneverseri par unke is kisse ko jaanate hai

 dev sahab ne esady burman or shailendra se apni film kaala bazaar main kaam karne ke liye approach kiya or unhone sweekaar kar liya

 ek din shailendra, esady burman se milane pahunche
 Burman tells him that a tune of the song has been prepared and he should write the song on it
 shailendra ne kaha ki wo jaldi hi gaanaa likhenge
 Many days passed, but Shailendra did not write the song
 burman da naaraaz ho gaye or unhen laga ki shailendra ghamandi ho gaye hai
 Now he did not want to say anything to Shailendra himself, so he told his son RD Burman (pancham da) that he somehow got Shailendra to write a song
 isi silsle main ek din shailendra or pancham da baithe hue the
 During the conversation, when Pancham mentioned the song, Shailendra said, i should write the song, but the idea is not coming the way i want
 is par pancham ne shailendra ko bataaya ki pita aapse naaraaz hai
 Shailendra ignored the matter and kept losing himself in the sky
 kuch der yun hi baithe baithe vah kuch budbudane lage
 Looking at the fifth, Shailendra said, "pancham tum jaat hai khonis ki nahin ki jaye hain chanting jaao jaye hain
" iske baad shailendra ne apni diary nikaali or geet likhnaa shuru kiya, 'khoyaa khoyaa chand, khulaa aasmaan, ankhon main sari raat jaaegi, tumko bhi kaise neend aegi
 "in the next few minutes, Shailendra wrote four songs and composed them

 aise main yadi beijing bharat kii koshish main phir se adnga nahin lagaataa he to pathankot hamale ke mastermind ko pratibandhit kiya ja sakegaa
 On 31 March this year, India's attempt to impose sanctions against jaish-e-mohammed under the UN Security Council sanctions committee was interrupted by a permanent veto-empowered member of China
 pandrah sadasyeey suraksha parishad main china hi ekmaatr aisa desh tha, jisane bharat ke aavedan par adnga lagaaya tha, jabaki sabhi 14 anya sadasyon ne ajahar kaa naam 1267 pratibandh suchi main daalane ke liye bharat ke prayaas kaa samarthan kiya tha
 Once Azhar's name appears in this ban list, his assets will be confiscated and travel ban will be imposed on him
 sutron ne bataaya ki takneekee adnge kii chah maheene kii vaidhata lagbhag ek saptaah
 
 10 din main 'khatm' hone vaali he or yadi china dobaaraa se kisi bahaane prastaav par roak kii maang nahin karata yaa vito kaa istemaal nahin karata to ajahar ko aatankwaadi ghoshit karne kii maang vaala bharat kaa prastaav swat: paarit ho saktaa he
 14 other members of the UN Security Council have already supported India's effort, and the end of the technical hurdle and no objection from China will necessarily mean Azhar's name in the sanctions list There is no opposition to the demand for pouring
 sutron ne kaha, 'aatankwaad ke khilaaf puri duniya main bad rahe aakrosh' ke maujuuda maahaul main 'kya china khud ko alag-thalag rakh saktaa he' or kya vah ek aise aadmi ko aatankwaadi ghoshit karaane kii koshish ko roak saktaa he jo aise sanghathan kaa sargana he jise sanyukt raashtra ne 2001 main aatanki sanghathan ghoshit kiya tha
 ' unhone kaha ki ek sambhaavna yah ho sakati he ki takneekee adnge kii avadhi khatm hone ke baad china ajahar se sambandhit aavedan par or samay maang saktaa he, jisase ki takneekee adnga jari rah sake
 However, other members of the UN Security Council may question China about this
 sutron ne kaha ki suraksha parishad ke anya sadsy china se puch sakate hai ki uske takneekee adnge kii vajah se chah maheene kii avadhi milane ke baad use or samay kyon chahie
 He said that India is not alone in trying to declare Azhar a terrorist from the United Nations Security Council as the US, Britain and France had 'co-sponsored' the proposal to declare Azhar a terrorist
 vartmaan sanyukt raashtra mahasabha satr main 140 se adhik deshon ne aam charchaa main apane sambodhan main aatankwaad kii kadi ninda kii he or isse ladane kaa sankalp vyakt kiya he
 Sources said whether in this situation any country (china) decided to go against the 'global consensus' on strengthening efforts in the fight against terrorism by maintaining its stubbornness and imposing an attempt to declare Azhar a terrorist
 Could? India has repeatedly reprimanded the United Nations Sanctions Committee for not mentioning the name of terrorists on the sanctions list, saying it was a 'flaw' and 'completely flawed' that terrorist groups would have been named in the sanctions committee
 , But the names of the donors of these groups are not included
 sutron ne kaha, 'kya osama bin laden alqaida se alag he, kya ve alqaida kaa naam pratibandh suchi main shaamil kar sakate hai or laden kaa nahin
 Syed Akbaruddin, India's permanent representative to the United Nations, said in June this year that it was 'completely flawed' that the new leader of the banned Taliban, Mawlawi Habtullah Akhundzadi, had not yet been named as a terrorist
 isse pehle bharat ne ajahar kaa naam pratibandh samiti main aatanki ke rup main darj karaane ke apane aavedan par takneekee adnga lagaae jane ke samay 'chuninda drushtikon' apnaane par samiti kii ninda kii thi
 India said in April that it felt 'incomprehensible' that Pakistan-based jaish-e-mohammed had been named by the UN Security Council in its sanctions list in 2001 for its terrorist activities and ties with Al Qaeda
 , But the leader of the group, the financier and the person tricking people for terrorist activities, has been named on the technical hurdle
 tippaniyan India had given a detailed dossier about Azhar and placed it before the 1267 Committee of the United Nations Security Council after the January 2 Pathankot attack, but China put a technical bottleneck in it and thus named Azhar in the ban list
 Could not be inserted nai dilli ne kaha tha ki pratibandh samiti aatankwaad se ladaai ke maamle main 'chuninda drushtikon' apana rahi he
 India had given a strong call for reforms, citing lack of transparency in its functioning
 (hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) is saal 31 march ko jaish-e-mohammad ke sargana par sanyukt raashtra suraksha parishad kii pratibandh samiti ke antargat pratibandh lagavane ke bharat kii koshish ko parishad ke vito adhikaar praapt sthai sadsy china ne baadhit kar diya tha
 China was the only country in the fifteen-member Security Council to put a cap on India's application, while all 14 other members supported India's effort to put Azhar's name on the 1267 ban list
 ajahar kaa naam is pratibandh suchi main aa jane par uski sampattiyon ko jabt kiya ja sakegaa or us par yatra pratibandh lag jayega
 Sources said the six-month validity of the technical bottleneck is about a week
 
 In 10 days 'will be over' and if China does not demand a restriction on any pretext or use the veto, then India's proposal to declare Azhar a terrorist may be automatically passed
 sanyukt raashtra suraksha parishad ke 14 anya sadsy pehle hi bharat ke prayaas kaa samarthan kar chuke hai or takneekee adnge kii avadhi khatm hone tathaa china kii taraf se dobaaraa koi aapatti nahin kiye jane kaa aavashyak rup se yah matlab hoga ki ajahar kaa naam pratibandh suchi main daalane kii maang kaa koi virodh nahin he
 In the current atmosphere of 'growing anger against terrorism all over the world', the sources said, 'can China isolate itself' and can it stop trying to declare a man who is such a terrorist? Is the kingpin of which was declared a terrorist organization by the United Nations in 2001
 ' He said that one possibility could be that after the end of the technical bottleneck, China could ask for more time on the application related to Azhar, so that the technical bottleneck could continue
 haalanki sanyukt raashtra suraksha parishad ke anya sadsy china se is bare main sawaal kar sakate hai
 Sources said that other members of the Security Council could ask China why it needed more time after a six-month period due to its technical bottlenecks
 unhone kaha ki ajahar ko sanyukt raashtra suraksha parishad se aatanki ghoshit karaane kii koshish main bharat akelaa nahin he kyonki america, britain or france ne ajahar ko aatanki ghoshit karaane ke prastaav ko 'sah-pryojit' kiya tha
 In the current UN General Assembly session, more than 140 countries have strongly condemned terrorism in their address and expressed their resolve to fight it
 sutron ne kaha ki kya is sthiti main koi desh (china) apni hath par kaayam rahakar or ajahar ko aatankwaadi ghoshit karaane ke prayaas main adnga lagaakar aatankwaad ke khilaaf ladaai kii koshishon ko majboot karne par 'vaishvik aam sahmati' ke khilaaf jane kaa faisla kar saktaa he? aatankwaadiyon kaa naam pratibandh suchi main na daale jane par bharat ne baar-baar sanyukt raashtra pratibandh samiti kii yah kahkar ninda kii he ki yah ek 'khami' or 'puri tarah trutipurna' he ki pratibandh samiti main aatankwaadi samoohon kaa naam to shaamil kiya jaataa he, lekin in samoohon ke sarganaon kaa naam shaamil nahin kiya jaataa
 Sources said, 'is Osama bin Laden different from Al Qaeda, can they include Al Qaeda's name in the ban list and not Laden's
 ' sanyukt raashtra main bharat ke sthai pratinidhi saiyad akbaruddin ne is saal june main kaha tha ki yah 'puri tarah trutipurna' he ki pratibandhit sanghathan taliban ke nae netaa mavalavi haibatulla akhundzaadi kaa naam ab tak aatanki vyakti ke rup main shaamil nahin kiya gaya he
 Earlier, India had slammed the committee for adopting a 'selective approach' at the time of putting technical constraints on its application to register Azhar's name as a terrorist in the ban committee
 bharat ne april main kaha tha ki use yah 'samaj se baahar' lagata he ki pakistan sthit jaish-e-mohammad kaa naam to sanyukt raashtra suraksha parishad ne uski aatanki gatividhiyon or alqaida se sambandhon ke liye 2001 main hi pratibandh suchi main daal diya tha, lekin samooh ke sargana, vittaposhak or logon ko aatanki gatividhiyon ke liye bargalane vaale vyakti ke naam ko takneekee adnge par rakhaa gaya he
 The comments bharat ne ajahar ke bare main ek vistrut dogier diya tha or do janvari ke pathankot hamale ke baad ise sanyukt raashtra suraksha parishad kii 1267 samiti ke samaksh rakhaa tha, lekin china ne isamen takneekee adnga laga diya tha or is tarah ajahar kaa naam pratibandh suchi main nahin daalaa ja sakaa tha
 New Delhi had said that the sanctions committee was adopting a 'selective approach' in the fight against terrorism
 isaki karypranali main paardarshita kii kami bataate hue bharat ne sudhaaron kaa majboot aahvaan kiya tha
 (apart from the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it has been published directly from the Syndicate feed

 The Board of Control for Cricket in India has decided to suspend the five cricket players with immediate effect for 15 days, whose name is related to the latest spot-fixing case

 unhen koi atirikt dhan nahin diya gaya he
 He has also apologized for saying so
 indian premier lig (ipel) ke kamishnar rajeev shukla ne mangalvaar ko yah jaankaree di
 These players have been shown talking about intentionally throwing no balls in a sting operation conducted by a television channel
 is sambandh main bisisiai ne jo jaanch shuru kii he, uski samiti ke pramukh purv sibiai adhikari ravi savani ne kaha, "bisisiai ne paanch khilaadiyon ko jaanch puri hone tak nilambit kar diya he
 We have to submit the report to the board within 15 to 20 days and during this time these players will remain suspended
 " Savani has previously served as the chairman of the icc's anti-corruption Unit
 savani ne bataaya ki nilambit kiye gaye khilaadi tipi sudhindra (deccan chargers), mohanish mishra (pune warirs), amit yadav (kings ilevan), shalab shrivastav (kings ilevan) or abhinav bali (dilli) shaamil hai
 Earlier, it was recommended to suspend five IPL cricketers who were in the grip of a sting operation aimed at exposing spot-fixing in cricket by a private TV channel
 sutron se mili is khabar ke mutabik ipel gavarning council ne yah faisla kiya tha
 On Tuesday itself, BJP leader and former cricketer Kirti Azad raised the matter in the Lok Sabha and demanded a strong action against the culprits after detailed investigation
 ullekhneey he ki is maamle main ek nijee tivi channel dwaara kiye gaye sting oparation main kul paanch khilaadiyon par aarope lagaae gaye hai
 Deccan Chargers fast bowler TP Sudhindra has asked for forty thousand rupees to bowl a no-ball in a home match
 itnaa hi nahin, isi sting oparation main kings ilevan ke shalab shrivastav bhi no-ball ke liye das lakh rupee maang rahe hai
 The TV channel claimed that it has uncovered 'suspicious deals' between players, organizers, owners and well-known people of Indian cricket in the IPL
 iske baad bisisiai ko chetavanee deni padi ki agar yah khabar sahi nikali to kadi karrwai kii jaaegi
 The TV channel claimed to have carried out a sting operation, in which several players were captured in hidden cameras, admitting that they had unauthorizedly received more money than was fixed at auction
 tippaniyan According to the channel, its operation revealed that spot-fixing is not only present in the IPL, but first-class matches are also fixed and women play an important role in match-fixing
 channel ne ek bayaan main kaha ki bhartiya cricket ke superstar or yahaan tak ki ek team kaa captain antarrashtriya khilaadi bhi in maichon ko fiks karne main mila hua he

 hamen 15 se 20 dinon ke bheetar report board ko saunpny he or is dauraan ye khilaadi nilambit rahenge
 " savani isse pehle isisi kii bhrashtachar nirodhi ikai ke adhyaksh ke taur par kaam kar chuke hai

 isse pehle, ek nijee tivi channel dwaara cricket main spot phixing ko ujagar karne ke uddeshy se kiye gaye sting oparation kii chapet main aae paanch ipel cricketron ko suspend karne kii sifarish kar di gai thi
 According to this news from sources, the decision was taken by IPL Governing Council
